<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Brazilian_Navy_today">Brazilian Navy today</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Brazilian Navy today">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Personnel">Personnel</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Personnel">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As of 2011, the Brazilian Navy has a reported strength of 60,000 active personnel,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58"><a href="#cite_note-58">[57]</a></sup> of which approximately 15,000 are naval infantry. The current Navy Commander is Admiral <a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=Eduardo_Leal_Ferreira&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="Eduardo Leal Ferreira (page does not exist)">Eduardo Leal Ferreira</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59"><a href="#cite_note-59">[58]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ships_and_submarines">Ships and submarines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Ships and submarines">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/List_of_ships_of_the_Brazilian_Navy" title="List of ships of the Brazilian Navy">List of ships of the Brazilian Navy</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sao_Paulo_carrier.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1800" data-file-width="2400" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Sao_Paulo_carrier.jpg/220px-Sao_Paulo_carrier.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Sao_Paulo_carrier.jpg/330px-Sao_Paulo_carrier.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Sao_Paulo_carrier.jpg/440px-Sao_Paulo_carrier.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sao_Paulo_carrier.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
lThe aircraft carrier <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_aircraft_carrier_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_(A12)" title="Brazilian aircraft carrier São Paulo (A12)"><i>São Paulo</i></a>.</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:AF1_da_Marinha_do_Brasil_2.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="521" data-file-width="800" height="143" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/AF1_da_Marinha_do_Brasil_2.jpg/220px-AF1_da_Marinha_do_Brasil_2.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/AF1_da_Marinha_do_Brasil_2.jpg/330px-AF1_da_Marinha_do_Brasil_2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/AF1_da_Marinha_do_Brasil_2.jpg/440px-AF1_da_Marinha_do_Brasil_2.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:AF1_da_Marinha_do_Brasil_2.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
An <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/McDonnell_Douglas_A-4_Skyhawk" title="McDonnell Douglas A-4 Skyhawk">AF-1 Skyhawk</a> of the Brazilian Navy.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>As of 2012, the Brazilian Navy had about 100 <a href="/wiki/Ship_commissioning" title="Ship commissioning">commissioned</a> ships,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Meios_Operativos:_Navios_60-0"><a href="#cite_note-Meios_Operativos:_Navios-60">[59]</a></sup> with others undergoing construction, acquisition and modernization. Between 1996 and 2005 the Navy retired 21 ships.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61"><a href="#cite_note-61">[60]</a></sup> The Brazilian Navy operated one <a href="/wiki/Clemenceau-class_aircraft_carrier" title="Clemenceau-class aircraft carrier"><i>Clemenceau</i>-class</a> aircraft carrier, <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_aircraft_carrier_S%C3%A3o_Paulo_(A12)" title="Brazilian aircraft carrier São Paulo (A12)"><i>São Paulo</i></a>, formerly the <a href="/wiki/French_Navy" title="French Navy">French Navy</a>'s <a href="/wiki/French_aircraft_carrier_Foch_(R99)" title="French aircraft carrier Foch (R99)"><i>Foch</i></a>. It was retired in 2017.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62"><a href="#cite_note-62">[61]</a></sup> Its possible replacements are presently in the early stage of planning and will not be expected until at least 2025.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63"><a href="#cite_note-63">[62]</a></sup></p>
<p>Four <i>Tupi</i>-class and one <i>Tikuna</i>-class <a href="/wiki/Type_209_submarine" title="Type 209 submarine">Type 209 submarines</a> are in the fleet. The <i>Tupi</i>-class submarines will be upgraded by <a href="/wiki/Lockheed_Martin" title="Lockheed Martin">Lockheed Martin</a> at a cost of $35 million.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64"><a href="#cite_note-64">[63]</a></sup> The modernization includes the replacement of existing <a href="/wiki/Torpedo" title="Torpedo">torpedoes</a> with new <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MK_48" title="MK 48">MK 48</a> units.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65"><a href="#cite_note-65">[64]</a></sup> On 14 March 2008, the Navy purchased four <a href="/wiki/Scorp%C3%A8ne-class_submarine" title="Scorpène-class submarine">Scorpène-class</a> submarines from <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">France</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66"><a href="#cite_note-66">[65]</a></sup> The Navy is currently developing its first <a href="/wiki/Nuclear_submarine" title="Nuclear submarine">nuclear submarine</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67"><a href="#cite_note-67">[66]</a></sup> The Navy plans to have the Scorpène-class submarines in service in 2017, and their first nuclear-powered submarine commissioned in 2023.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68"><a href="#cite_note-68">[67]</a></sup></p>
<p>In August 2008 the Navy incorporated the <a href="/wiki/Corvette" title="Corvette">corvette</a> <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_corvette_Barroso_(V34)" title="Brazilian corvette Barroso (V34)"><i>Barroso</i></a>, which was designed and built in Brazil<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69"><a href="#cite_note-69">[68]</a></sup> at a cost of $263 million.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70"><a href="#cite_note-70">[69]</a></sup> In August 2012 the Navy requested 4 new ships based on the <i>Barroso</i> class but redesigned using a stealth design.</p>
<p>The PROSUPER program plans to acquire, firstly, five new 6,000-ton frigates, five new <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Offshore_patrol_vessel" title="Offshore patrol vessel">offshore patrol vessels</a> and one Logistics Support Vessel.</p>
<p>In January 2012 <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems" title="BAE Systems">BAE Systems</a> contracted to supply three patrol vessels that were <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Port_of_Spain-class_corvette" title="Port of Spain-class corvette"><i>Port of Spain</i>-class</a> corvettes. The contract is worth £133m. The offshore patrol vessels are already built, originally ordered by the government of <a href="/wiki/Trinidad_and_Tobago" title="Trinidad and Tobago">Trinidad and Tobago</a> in a contract which was terminated in 2010.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-71"><a href="#cite_note-71">[70]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72"><a href="#cite_note-72">[71]</a></sup> The first vessel was commissioned at the end of June 2012, the second was scheduled for December 2012 and the last in April 2013.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73"><a href="#cite_note-73">[72]</a></sup></p>
<p>In March 2014, the Brazilian Navy announced plans to domestically build an aircraft carrier, with plans to enter service around 2029. Originally, <i>São Paulo</i> was to be modernized until its introduction, but escalating repair costs forced its retirement in February 2017. The carrier will likely be based on an existing project and be built with a foreign partner. French company <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/DCNS_(company)" title="DCNS (company)">DCNS</a> has a strong presence in Brazil and is already engaged in building five submarines and a naval base in the country. The company has been showcasing their DEAC Aircraft Carrier project based on the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/French_aircraft_carrier_Charles_de_Gaulle_(R91)" title="French aircraft carrier Charles de Gaulle (R91)"><i>Charles de Gaulle</i></a> carrier's design and aviation systems including launching conventional take-off aircraft, <a href="/wiki/Unmanned_aerial_vehicle" title="Unmanned aerial vehicle">unmanned aerial vehicle</a> integration, advanced conventional propulsion, and platform stabilization systems. American company <a href="/wiki/General_Atomics" title="General Atomics">General Atomics</a> is marketing their <a href="/wiki/Electromagnetic_Aircraft_Launch_System" title="Electromagnetic Aircraft Launch System">Electromagnetic Aircraft Launch System (EMALS)</a> to Brazil. Possible aircraft to be operated by the carrier may include the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saab_Gripen" title="Saab Gripen">Saab Sea Gripen</a>, given that the Air Force has chosen the land-based version as their new jet fighter.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74"><a href="#cite_note-74">[73]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Aircraft">Aircraft</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Aircraft">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>As of 2011, the <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Naval_Aviation" title="Brazilian Naval Aviation">Naval Aviation</a> arm of the Navy operates around 85 aircraft. All the aircraft, with the exception of the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/A-4_Skyhawk" title="A-4 Skyhawk">A-4 Skyhawks</a>, are <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Helicopters" title="Helicopters">helicopters</a>.</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marines">Marines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Marines">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Marine_Corps" title="Brazilian Marine Corps">Brazilian Marine Corps</a> (<a href="/wiki/Portuguese_language" title="Portuguese language">Portuguese</a>: <b>Corpo de Fuzileiros Navais</b>; <b>CFN</b>)<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75"><a href="#cite_note-75">[74]</a></sup> is the land combat branch of the Brazilian Navy.</p>
<div style="clear:both;"></div>
<ul class="gallery mw-gallery-packed">
<li class="gallerybox" style="width: 182px">
<div style="width: 182px">

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Structure_and_organisation">Structure and organisation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: Structure and organisation">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Branches">Branches</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Branches">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:BNS_Rademaker_F49.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1500" data-file-width="2100" height="157" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/BNS_Rademaker_F49.jpg/220px-BNS_Rademaker_F49.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/BNS_Rademaker_F49.jpg/330px-BNS_Rademaker_F49.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/BNS_Rademaker_F49.jpg/440px-BNS_Rademaker_F49.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:BNS_Rademaker_F49.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The Type 22 frigate <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brazilian_frigate_Rademaker_(F49)" title="Brazilian frigate Rademaker (F49)"><i>Rademaker</i></a></div>
</div>
</div>
<p>The main branches of the Brazilian Navy are:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76"><a href="#cite_note-76">[75]</a></sup></p>
<ul>
<li>The "<i>Comando de Operações Navais</i>" (Naval Operations Command)
<ul>
<li>The "<i>Comando da Força de Superfície</i>" (Surface Fleet Command)</li>
<li>The "<i>Comando da Força de Submarinos</i>" (Submarine Fleet Command)</li>
<li>The "<i><a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Naval_Aviation" title="Brazilian Naval Aviation">Comando da Força Aeronaval</a></i>" (Naval Aviation Command)</li>
<li>The "<i>Comando da 1ª Divisão da Esquadra</i>" (1st Fleet Division Command)</li>
<li>The "<i>Comando da 2ª Divisão da Esquadra</i>" (2nd Fleet Division Command)</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>The "<a href="/wiki/Brazilian_Marine_Corps" title="Brazilian Marine Corps"><i>Comando Geral do Corpo de Fuzileiros Navais</i></a>" (Marine Corps General Command)</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Naval_Districts">Naval Districts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Naval Districts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_110422-N-ZI300-115_The_Brazilian_navy_frigate_Bosisio_(F_48)_fires_at_an_unmanned_aerial_vehicle_during_a_drone_exercise_(DRONEX)_with_ship.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2465" data-file-width="3451" height="157" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/US_Navy_110422-N-ZI300-115_The_Brazilian_navy_frigate_Bosisio_%28F_48%29_fires_at_an_unmanned_aerial_vehicle_during_a_drone_exercise_%28DRONEX%29_with_ship.jpg/220px-US_Navy_110422-N-ZI300-115_The_Brazilian_navy_frigate_Bosisio_%28F_48%29_fires_at_an_unmanned_aerial_vehicle_during_a_drone_exercise_%28DRONEX%29_with_ship.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/US_Navy_110422-N-ZI300-115_The_Brazilian_navy_frigate_Bosisio_%28F_48%29_fires_at_an_unmanned_aerial_vehicle_during_a_drone_exercise_%28DRONEX%29_with_ship.jpg/330px-US_Navy_110422-N-ZI300-115_The_Brazilian_navy_frigate_Bosisio_%28F_48%29_fires_at_an_unmanned_aerial_vehicle_during_a_drone_exercise_%28DRONEX%29_with_ship.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/02/US_Navy_110422-N-ZI300-115_The_Brazilian_navy_frigate_Bosisio_%28F_48%29_fires_at_an_unmanned_aerial_vehicle_during_a_drone_exercise_%28DRONEX%29_with_ship.jpg/440px-US_Navy_110422-N-ZI300-115_The_Brazilian_navy_frigate_Bosisio_%28F_48%29_fires_at_an_unmanned_aerial_vehicle_during_a_drone_exercise_%28DRONEX%29_with_ship.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:US_Navy_110422-N-ZI300-115_The_Brazilian_navy_frigate_Bosisio_(F_48)_fires_at_an_unmanned_aerial_vehicle_during_a_drone_exercise_(DRONEX)_with_ship.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
The Brazilian Navy frigate <i>Bosísio</i> fires at an unmanned aerial vehicle during a drone exercise (DRONEX) with ship.</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li>1º Distrito Naval da Marinha do Brasil (Rio de Janeiro-RJ)</li>
<li>2º Distrito Naval da Marinha do Brasil (Salvador-BA)</li>
<li>3º Distrito Naval da Marinha do Brasil (Natal-RN)</li>
<li>4º Distrito Naval da Marinha do Brasil (Belém-PA)</li>
<li>5º Distrito Naval da Marinha do Brasil (Rio Grande-RS)</li>
<li>6º Distrito Naval da Marinha do Brasil (Ladário-MS)</li>
<li>7º Distrito Naval da Marinha do Brasil (Brasilia-DF)</li>
<li>8º Distrito Naval da Marinha do Brasil (São Paulo-SP)</li>
<li>9º Distrito Naval da Marinha do Brasil (Manaus-AM)</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Naval_bases">Naval bases</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Naval bases">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Brazilian_navy_visit,_board,_search_and_seizure_(VBSS)_team.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1920" data-file-width="1494" height="283" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Brazilian_navy_visit%2C_board%2C_search_and_seizure_%28VBSS%29_team.jpg/220px-Brazilian_navy_visit%2C_board%2C_search_and_seizure_%28VBSS%29_team.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Brazilian_navy_visit%2C_board%2C_search_and_seizure_%28VBSS%29_team.jpg/330px-Brazilian_navy_visit%2C_board%2C_search_and_seizure_%28VBSS%29_team.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/Brazilian_navy_visit%2C_board%2C_search_and_seizure_%28VBSS%29_team.jpg/440px-Brazilian_navy_visit%2C_board%2C_search_and_seizure_%28VBSS%29_team.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Brazilian_navy_visit,_board,_search_and_seizure_(VBSS)_team.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
A <a href="/wiki/GRUMEC" title="GRUMEC">GRUMEC</a> visit, board, search, and seizure (VBSS) team attached to the frigate <i>Independência</i> conducts a simulated boarding operation.</div>
</div>
</div>
<p>As of 2009, the main naval bases in use are:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77"><a href="#cite_note-77">[76]</a></sup></p>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rio_de_Janeiro_(state)" title="Rio de Janeiro (state)">Rio de Janeiro</a>:
<ul>
<li>"<i>Base Naval Almirante Castro e Silva</i>", submarine base</li>
<li>"<i>Base Naval do Rio de Janeiro</i>", main naval base</li>
<li>"<i>Arsenal da Marinha do Rio de Janeiro</i>", naval shipyard</li>
<li>"<i>Base Aérea Naval de São Pedro da Aldeia</i>", naval aviation base</li>
<li>"<i>Base de Fuzileiros Navais da Ilha do Governador</i>", marine corps base</li>
<li>"<i>Base de Fuzileiros Navais da Ilha das Flores</i>", marine corps base</li>
<li>"<i>Base de Fuzileiros Navais do Rio Meriti</i>", marine corps base</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Bahia" title="Bahia">Bahia</a>:
<ul>
<li>"<i>Base Naval de Aratu</i>", naval base and repair facility</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rio_Grande_do_Norte" title="Rio Grande do Norte">Rio Grande do Norte</a>:
<ul>
<li>"<i>Base Naval de Natal</i>", naval base</li>
<li>"<i>Base Naval Almirante Ary Parreiras</i>", naval base and repair facility</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Par%C3%A1" title="Pará">Pará</a>:
<ul>
<li>"<i>Base Naval de Val-de-Cães</i>", naval base and repair facility</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Mato_Grosso_do_Sul" title="Mato Grosso do Sul">Mato Grosso do Sul</a>:
<ul>
<li>"<i>Base Fluvial de Ladário</i>", <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Riverine" title="Riverine">riverine</a> naval aviation base, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Riverine" title="Riverine">riverine</a> naval base and repair facility</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Amazonas_(Brazilian_state)" title="Amazonas (Brazilian state)">Amazonas</a>:
<ul>
<li>"<i>Estação Naval do Rio Negro</i>", <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Riverine" title="Riverine">riverine</a> naval base and repair facility</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Rio_Grande_do_Sul" title="Rio Grande do Sul">Rio Grande do Sul</a>:
<ul>
<li>"<i>Estação Naval do Rio Grande</i>", naval base</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Brazilian_Navy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: upper-alpha;">
<div class="mw-references-wrap">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-40"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-40">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">A professional diplomat and the son of the famed <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Paranhos,_Viscount_of_Rio_Branco" title="José Paranhos, Viscount of Rio Branco">Viscount of Rio Braco</a>, the Baron of Rio Branco was named as Brazil's <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Foreign_Minister_of_Brazil" title="Foreign Minister of Brazil">Foreign Minister</a> in 1902 after a distinguished career as a diplomat, and served there until his death in 1912. In that time, he oversaw the signing of many treaties and mediated territorial disputes between Brazil and its neighbors, and became a famous name in his own right.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39"><a href="#cite_note-39">[39]</a></sup></span></li>
</ol>
</div>
</div>
